1b1(phal chen): shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo sangs rgyas phal po che zhes
1b2(phal chen): bya ba/ bam po dang po// dum bu bzhi pa/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' tshogs
1b3(phal chen): chen po de'i nang nas byang chub sems dpa' kha cig 'di snyam du sems te/ sangs
1b4(phal chen): rgyus bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing ni ci tsam zhig du bsam gyis
1b5(phal chen): mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sngon gyi smon lam dang 'byung ba
2a1(phal chen): rnam par dag pa ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin
2a2(phal chen): gshegs pa'i sku gdung ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas skye ban
2a3(phal chen): ma zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku ni ji tsam zhig du bas
2a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab
2a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas
2a6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas
2b1(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa mi mnga' ba'i rnam par spyod pa ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam pa
2b2(phal chen): zar pa ni ji tsam zhig du bsam gyis mi khyab snyam pa dang / de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag gi sems mkhyen pas thugs su chud nas/ byang chub sems
2b3(phal chen): dpa' ud pa la'i snying po// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis byin du brlabs so// sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyis byin dang ldan par mdzad do// de bzhin gra shegs pa'i 'od
2b4(phal chen): snang ba mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi gzi brjid kyis yongs su rgyas par mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi mi 'jigs pa la rab tu bzhag go/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa
2b5(phal chen): yodu chud par mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba nyid dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi yul rab tu rtogs par mdzad do// chags pa med pa'i rgyud 'byam klas pa la rab tu bzhag go/ 
2b6(phal chen): yangs rgyas thams cad gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i rigs rab tu shegs par mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi tshul gyi gnas brjod du med pa la rab tu gzhag pa mdzad do// de nas bya
2b7(phal chen): chub sems dpa' ud pa la'i snying pos chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa reg cing khong du chud pas chags pa med pa'i dbyings su sgrub pa'i yid dang / chos thams cad la sgrib pa med pa
2b8(phal chen): gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa dang / kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang ldan pa'i yang dag par 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su song ba'i sangs rgyas blta
3a1(phal chen): snying pos smra ba'i sems can thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i go ca chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yin ma dang / spyod pa'i dkyil la bar rgyun chad
3a2(phal chen): med bdag/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa skad cig gi tsho shes la rnam par spyod pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sgo mthong ba mi zang pa dang / so so yang dag pa
3a3(phal chen): dge pa'i rnam pa gzungs thams cad kyis snang bar byas pa dang ldan pas sangs rgyas kyis thus byang chub sems dpa' bad mo'i snying po la 'di skad ces smras so// 
3a4(phal chen): 'isras/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ tshad med pa la rnam par spyod pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par 'phrul pa chen
3a5(phal chen): rnam par spyod pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnabs ni sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa thams cad la/ sku'i mtshan thams cad rab tu brnyes pa'o// sangs
3a6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba ni ting nge 'dzin dang // dgongs pas sbyar ba'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi so so yang dag par rig pa ba' ni
3a7(phal chen): rjod du med pa yang brjod du shin tu bstan pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la bsam gyis mi khyab par spyod pa'o// sangs rgyas
3b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi khyu mchog gam nu byung ba na thams cad ma ngon par mkhyen pa 'o// tu rgyas pa sras dag/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis
3b2(phal chen): dbyings thugs su chud cing / bstan pa ni slob pa med pa'i mthar thug pa 'o// kye rgyas pa'i sras/ bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings mthar dang
3b3(phal chen): dbus med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku gzugs kyi rnam par dgu pa ni rtog pa med par rgyud thams cad du blang ba
3b4(phal chen): dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa med pa'i spyan ni chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi spyan mngon par sangs rgyas pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// 
3b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa med pa'i sman ni 'gro ba thams cad kyi sgra sgrib pa med par thugs su chud pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
3b6(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi shangs kyi skye mched ni sangs rgyas kyi bang 'thabs cad kyi rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shas
3b7(phal chen): skye mched ni sangs rgyas kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// langs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs shin tu yangs pa'i chos kyi dbyings rnams
3b8(phal chen): da du gsung gi dbyangs rjes su 'gro bas mtha' dang dbus
4a1(phal chen): lade bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba rnam par dmigs pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku dang tha yidad cing dus gsum
4a2(phal chen): chags pa med par thugs su chud cing rnam par shes pa dang rnam par dag pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par thar ba sgrib pa mi mnga'
4a3(phal chen): ba la rnam par spyod pa ni sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang dang rnam par 'phral ba dang / cho 'phrul mi zad pa yang dag par ston pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
4a4(phal chen): rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rnam par dag pa ni brjod du med pa'i rgyan byin gyis rarlabs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa yang dag par bstan te/ 
4a5(phal chen): sab pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par dmigs par mdzad pas mtha' dang dbus med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang / 
4a6(phal chen): smon lam thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa ni rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi chos yongs su rdzogs te/ chos thams cad rdzogs par byang chub par bya ba la mtha' dang dbus med pa ste/ 
4a7(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams
4a8(phal chen): so/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig la ye shes mngon par sgrub pa yang dag par bstan pa'o// bcu gang shes
4b1(phal chen): skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dga' ldan gyi gnas nas 'pho ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du byang chub sems
4b2(phal chen): dpa'i tshe longs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcigs 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du mngon par 'byung ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig sa 'jig rter gyi khams rnams
4b3(phal chen): dadu bzhugs shing mngon par 'tshang rgyab yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gi cig lnga 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du chos kyi 'khor mo bskor ba yongs su/ 
4b4(phal chen): bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'dul ba'i sems can yongs su smin pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du/ dus la bab pa shes pas sangs rgyas bsnyen bkun
4b5(phal chen): ba yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du sems can ji ltar 'dul ba'i tshul bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa brjod du med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi
4b6(phal chen): sku sna tshogs rnam par dmigs pa yongs su bstan pa dang skud cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du/ rgyan sna tshogs dang rgyan brjod du med pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
4b7(phal chen): tshig gi mthu byung ba dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod yongs su bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rnam par dag pa gcig ma yin pa thams cad/ 
4b8(phal chen): stan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad du dbang po dang / brtson 'grus
5a1(phal chen): rnam pa tha dad pa byung ba dang / mos pa dang / spyod pa rnam pa tha dang 'a byung ba las dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyud mngon par 'tshang rgya ba yongs su bstan pa ste/ 
5a2(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad ceg la ye shes mngon par bsgrub pa yang dag par bstan pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po/ 
5a3(phal chen): 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da' ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mngon par 'tshang rgya ba ni/ de'i dus
5a4(phal chen): las ma 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dge ba rnam par smin pa dang / rnam par smin pa mnyam pa nyid ni de'i dus las yi 'dra' bas dus la
5a5(phal chen): ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can gyi bsam pa yongs su smin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams lung bstan pa ni de'i dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas
5a6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can khri bsam pa'i rgyud du/ cho 'phrul yongs su bsnun pa ni de'i dus la mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnas/ 
5a7(phal chen): sa sems can mos pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sku yongs su bstan pa de ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams btang
5a8(phal chen): yos su bzhugs pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams yul dang / grong dang / krong brdal du gshegs pa de ni de'i dus
5b1(phal chen): 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dad pa jes bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can yongs su 'dzin pa na/ de'i dus las ma 'da' bas dus
5b2(phal chen): la bab yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can kun nas nyor mongs pa dang ldan ning gdul dka' ba lnga gzhan la ltos pa mi mnga' bar 'dul ba ni de'i dus la sna
5b3(phal chen): 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas/ rnam par 'phrul pa bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi 'ad
5b4(phal chen): bas dus la bab pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dge ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rabs kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus la sa mi 'da' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni spangs
5b5(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par skyel mo krung ka cig gis
5b6(phal chen): rgyas par dgang ba dang / dus cig tu sangs rgyas thams cad yongs su bstad pa dang / 'dog zer gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad snang bar bya ba dang / sdu gzugs
5b7(phal chen): cig gis lus dang / gzugs thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / gnas gcig na bzhugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par byon pa'i skur 'gyur ba dang / ye
5b8(phal chen): thams cad la sgrib ba med par 'gyur ba dang / thugs gcig bskyed pas chos kyi
6a1(phal chen): che ba nyid tshad med pa dang ldan pa'i gshegs stabs gcig gis de kho na nyid yang dag par bstan pa dang / dus gsum thams cad sangs rgyas TI go 'phang gis rgyas par/ 
6a2(phal chen): 'gengs pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad dngas 'dres par bzhugs shing 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar blang ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang / mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis
6a3(phal chen): tad kyi tshul gcig pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sas bcu po de dge ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i grang
6a4(phal chen): rgya bo 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlab mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/ bcug bsnyen/ 'jug pa med pa'i chos thams cad la 'jug pas
6a5(phal chen): nolam mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / lus med pa la lus mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad mi gnyis pa la mngon par 'tshang rgya ba mngon par bsgrub
6a6(phal chen): we shes dang / sem can gyi mthar thug par bdag med pa lnga sems can 'dul bar mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / rjes thams cad mtshan ma sna tshogs mngon par
6a7(phal chen): pa'i ye shes dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul ma skyes pa la 'jig rten gyi khams 'du ba dang / 'jig pa mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang / yul thams cad mngon par 'du bya
6a8(phal chen): de pa la las kyi rnam par smin pa mngon par bslab pa'i ye shes dang / ches thams cad brjod du med pa la/ chos kyi dbyings su gsung mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes dang mos
6b1(phal chen): thams cad kun nas nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang bas 'jug pa med pa la kun nas sngon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba mngon par bslab pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad ma skyes pa
6b2(phal chen): la skye ba dang / 'jig rten pa'i mtshan nyid rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba mngon par bsgrub pa'i ye shes te/ rgyal ba'i sras bcu po dadag ni de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi mngon par bsdu
6b3(phal chen): ba'i ye shes so// kye rgyas pa'i snas bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa'i khongs su rbad pa dag ste/ bcu gang zhed/ sangs chas bcom ldan 'das na mong
6b4(phal chen): ku ni dus gsum thams cad kyi rjes su 'brang ba'i khongs su drud ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can thams cad 'dul bar mdzad pa ni/ cho 'phrul chen po gsum/ 
6b5(phal chen): yongs su rung ba yid/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams tshig rab tu dbye ba thams cad la mkhas pa ni sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi gzungs thams cad kyi khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas
6b6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo thams cad ni de ba'i ra gshegs pa'i bo so yang dag par rig pa pa ne'i yongs su chud pa bar/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can
6b7(phal chen): thams cad yongs su mi gtong ba ni thugs rje chen po'i khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams rtag tu mnyam par gzhag pa ni dus thams cad du sems can thams dang
6b8(phal chen): gas pa'i khongs su chud ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnabs kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba ni sems can rnam par 'dul ba thams cad khongs su chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas ba
7a1(phal chen): ldan 'das kyi chags 'asem pa bang spya man chos kyi dbyis mams car khongs du chud pa men/ sangs rgyas bac+doMs can 'dag rnams kyi ga rtsigagacigs ni 'das
7a2(phal chen): tsun pa /  sa rgya skye ldan na ma /  ma pan sa sa rnas kyi
7a3(phal chen): bsten pasems cad khongs su chud pa yin/ kye rgyal pa'i bras cu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshad med pa'i khongs su chud pa'o// me rgyul pa'i
7a4(phal chen): sras chu bo bdi dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba rnams te/ bcu gang zhen/ bdud kyi dkrugs mA rab tu 'joms nyid rnam
7a5(phal chen): bar 'thong ba ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan dam rnams kyi shin tu rgyu che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// mu stegs can gzhan dang bas kyi rgol ba tshor gcad pa ni sangs rgyas bcom
7a6(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i ches bzod par dka' ba'o// 'dul ba'i sems can thams cad rab tu tshim par mdzad pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shis
7a7(phal chen): che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// sems can 'dul ba'i dbang gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad tu gshegs pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu
7a8(phal chen): chos bzod par dka' ba'o// chos kyi dbyings bugras su chud pa'i ye shes ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// 'jig rten
7b1(phal chen): bya thams cad ma lus par smras khyab cing sangs rgyas kyi sku rnam par dbye ba sna tshogs thams cad du/ mi gnyis pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin sun can tham
7b2(phal chen): zod par dka' ba'o// gsung gi yan lag thams cad la sems can mos par bya ba dang / thos par bya ba dang / gdul bar bya ba don yod par yang dag par rig pa thogs pa med pas bsdu
7b3(phal chen): ba'i tshul du so so yang dag par rig pa bzhi 'byung ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi
7b4(phal chen): spu'i zug gcig nas de bzhin gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rje shin tu phrub skyed bsam gyis mi khyab cing / thogs pa med pa'i tshul du 'jig rten gyi khrims tham
7b5(phal chen): rigyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi thabs kyis 'byung zhing de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku'i ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas 'byung ba ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya
7b6(phal chen): chos bamod par dka' ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams tham
7b7(phal chen): dkyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi yongs su ston cing / sangs rgyas kyi rgyan dang rang bzhin gyi khyab lhub dang / chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba rgyun mi 'chad cing sems can rnam par 'dul ba thob
7b8(phal chen): ngab 'jig rten gyi sasu de dag tu gtugs pa rnams la 'ang mi bad ba dang / gnod pa med kyang dril shin tu phra ba de'ang yangs par ma byas/ 'jig rten gyi 'ams de dag kyang chung ba
8a1(phal chen): byas par ji ltar gnas pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyang thugs su chud pa'i ye shes mnga' ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par/ 
8a2(phal chen): dka' ba ro// mun pa med pa'i khams de bzhin gshegs pas mngon par sangs rgyas te/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mun pa med cing sgrib pa mi mnga' la sems can garol
8a3(phal chen): ba sna tshogs kyi gnas rnam par sel na/ de la de bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang ldan pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams shin tu rgya che ba'i cho
8a4(phal chen): yod par bka' ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag bcu po'i de dag
8a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yang dag
8a6(phal chen): gyi mtha' nas rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / 
8a7(phal chen): byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi chud du rigs dang ldan par 'byung ba'i bdag nyid che ba ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rnam par dag pas/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med ci
8a8(phal chen): shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par shes pa la miganas pa ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni
8b1(phal chen): sbyar thug par gnas pas/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing / shin tu rnam 'ar dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dus gsum la mi gnas par rnam par
8b2(phal chen): spyod cing chos thams cad la rten par yang dag par dgra bcom pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam
8b3(phal chen): blor dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po rnam patha dad pal rnam par gzhag pa gcig gis len pa med pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag
8b4(phal chen): nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mthar chos kyi dbyings la gnas pas/ 
8b5(phal chen): mnyam pa'i bsod nams mi bde ba dang ldan pas mi zad pa'i bsod nams mnga' ba ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing
8b6(phal chen): shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gzugs dang kha dog mtha' yas pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na sems can 'dul ba'i dus dang dang
8b7(phal chen): sa chags pa med par bzhugs pa sa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom
8b8(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni mi mjigs pa lazhi ba rnyes pas bag chang mi mnga' bar bzhugs shing // khyu mchog dang seng ge'i nga ra'i byin te rgol ba'i nang na stag ste bu mthu dang ldan pa la chos thams
9a1(phal chen): cad bstan pa thugs sman mo// bu mnga' bas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu
9a2(phal chen): blar dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas 'askal pa 'arjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa zhig lon yang mtshan gyi tshig zas pacas
9a3(phal chen): kyis bzhugs pa dang 'dra bar sems can rnams kyi yon tan shin tu stong zhing mya ngan las 'das nas de srid kyi yun ring po 'das kyang sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i yon tan zad par
9a4(phal chen): 'gyur bas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du khan ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
9a5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjid du med pa dag na bzhugs shing 'jig ter gyi khams rgyang ring pon bzhugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams 'di sems can rnams
9a6(phal chen): kyis rjes su dran par byas nas sku mngon par ston pa mdzad pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu ma
9a7(phal chen): dag pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i slas bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni rnam pa thams cad du kha na mtho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// kye rgya
9a8(phal chen): sras dag bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shen 'arnam par dag pa ste/ bcu yang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi tshangs pa'i spyod pa
9b1(phal chen): dam par dag pa la sngon gyi smon lam gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i tshul khrims kyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin
9b2(phal chen): ngas rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa sel bas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na sangs rgyas kyi zhing sa
9b3(phal chen): shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'khor gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rigs rnam par dag pas shin tu
9b4(phal chen): bar dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzugs kyi sku'i mtshan dang / dpe byad bzang po rnam par dag pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
9b5(phal chen): chos kyi klu rnyog pa med pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi phung po sgrib pa med pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin
9b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi rna par zang pa thams cad la mthu chen po rnyes shing / pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa brnyes pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin te/ kye rgyu
9b7(phal chen): 'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyasra bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa 'a
9b8(phal chen): rten gyi khams thams cad du 'byung zhing dus thams cad du gnas pa ste/ bcug pa zhe na/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pazer ba'i sems can rnams pa dus thams cad du sangs rgyas bstanapa
10a1(phal chen): sems can sems cad shas dang ldan pa rnams ga/ dus thams cad du chos bstan pa dang / sems can sangs rgyas la dad pa'i sems dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba
10a2(phal chen): dus thams cad du bskyed pa dang / chos kyang skyon med par 'das pa'i sems can rnams dus thams cad du ye shes khong du chud par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi mdzad
10a3(phal chen): ba dus thams cad du rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dus thams cad du/ chags pa mi mnga' bar gshegs pa dang / 
10a4(phal chen): sems can thams cad la thugs rje chen pos dus thams cad du mi gtong ba dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa
10a5(phal chen): du/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa sna tshogs dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos kyi
10a6(phal chen): dbyings gnas pa'i sangs rgyas dus thams cad 'byung ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po dadag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dus
10a7(phal chen): 'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'i tshul rnams te/ bcu gang
10a8(phal chen): der/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i bu ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi phrin las tshad med pas
10b1(phal chen): brnyes pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi spyan gyi gus mang rabs ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ 
10b2(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsal tshad med pa bsam gyis mi byab pa banga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho me zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi char mngon par 'bab pas ye shes rgya mtsho ba da
10b3(phal chen): ba'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan legs pa mang po mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho ma zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi ma ni
10b4(phal chen): srung thams cad mkhyen pa'i smon lam dang khyad par mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni phye ma'i mtha'i mur 'gro ba thams cad sangs rgyas kyi
10b5(phal chen): drin las rgyun me 'chad par sgrub pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi rigs thams cad ma lus pa'i sems dang spyod pa la ye
10b6(phal chen): shes rnamatsho me zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams zil gyis mi non pas ye shes rgya mtsho ma zad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po dag/ 
10b7(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho me zad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
10b8(phal chen): mas kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad kyis mngon par 'byung ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 
11a1(phal chen): 'di lta ste chos thams cad la mi mkhyen pa gang yang mi mnga' ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste chos thams cad kyang thugs rdza
11a2(phal chen): chen po dang ldan pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta skye thams cad kyang stobs bcu tshar med pa dang ldan pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
11a3(phal chen): dpas kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste thams cad kyang tha na med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu skor ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste thams cad/ 
11a4(phal chen): sems can 'dral ba la yang dag par zhugs pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste thams cad kyang 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du mngon par
11a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste 'dul ba'i sems can rnams 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan
11a6(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste mi gnyis par yang dag par 'od pa'i mtshan nyid kyis chos la rab tu gzhol ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 
11a7(phal chen): de lta ste ji ltar yongs su smin par 'gyur ba dang / dul bar 'gyur ba'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi yul mu med pas sangs rgyas kyi yongs su mya ngan las 'dar bstod pa 'di
11a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi tshul yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po bdag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul lo// kye rgyal pa'i sras bcu po 'di dag
11b1(phal chen): desangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgo rnams te/ bcu ga zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams shin tu
11b2(phal chen): stan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi spyod pa sna tshogs shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'ad
11b3(phal chen): zag ni sems can thams cad kyi las dang rnam par smin pa shin tu bstan pa'i slor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad la gdams
11b4(phal chen): payan ngag shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can mama' yas pa rnam pa stong ba'i nan tan gyi sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgya
11b5(phal chen): com ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa thams cad la gdams ngag dang man ngag gis yongs su gzhol ba'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
11b6(phal chen): dmas ni byang chub sems dpa' khyad par gyi smon lam rnam pa tha dad pas 'byung ba shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mapa' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi
11b7(phal chen): sa thams cad ma lus pa'i 'du ba dang 'jig pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa ni byang chub sems
11b8(phal chen): pa'i bsam pa dang mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs su bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du 'ad
12a1(phal chen): // dang / mabyon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas gcig nas gcigs brgyud pa na bskal ba yangs pa de dang de dag tu bstan cing brjod pa dang / yongs su bshad pas/ 
12a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi ye shes thams cad khong du chub par bya ba'i sbyor mtha' las pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos ma
12a3(phal chen): sa pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgo'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprin las sems can rnams la bsgrub pa ste/ bcug
12a4(phal chen): nen/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku yongs su bstan pa ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung
12a5(phal chen): yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bslab po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mang ba yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bslab po
12a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mi mdzad pa yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bskur po// sa dang chu dang sde dang / rlung gis kyang sangs rgyas bcom
12a7(phal chen): na 'das rnams sems can rnams pa sangs rgyas kyi drin las bsgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byin gyis brlabs kyi yul dang yi dmigs pa thams cad yul
12a8(phal chen): mdzad pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bslab po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mtshan kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
12b1(phal chen): bsgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni zhing la dmigs par mdzad pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
12b2(phal chen): rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub bo// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mi gsung bar bzhugs pa yang
12b3(phal chen): sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sems can rnams la bslu
12b4(phal chen): ba'o// // bam po gnyis pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gartson 'chos te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sman las chen po la
12b5(phal chen): tu brten zhing smon lam zhig pa mi mnga' bas ji skad du gsung ba de ltar mdzad cing gnyis su mi gsung ba 'di ni sems can gyig tso ba'i chos dang po'o// phyi ma'i mtha'i mung thug pa'i bsku
12b6(phal chen): pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la yon tan thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad pas rab tu brtson zhing sgyid lug pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni sems can gyi gzo ba'i chos
12b7(phal chen): gnyis pa'o// sems can 'dul bar 'gyur ba gcig gcig gzigs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par gshegs shing 'jig rten gyi khams thams
12b8(phal chen): ngang gshegs pa la thag thogs med pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos gsum pa'o// zhe sdang ba'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa dang / dad pa'i sems can
13a1(phal chen): rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa 'di ni sems can gyig tso ba'i chos bzhi pa'o// gang gi tshe bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhum
13a2(phal chen): nas/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas kyi bar du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su mi 'gyur ro// 
13a3(phal chen): sum du byang chub kyi sems ma nyams pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso ba 'jos lnga pa'o// dge ba'i rtsub thams cad yang dag par bsgrub cing / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su
13a4(phal chen): bsngo bas 'jug gi// 'jig rten pa'i rgyud la ma yin pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i ches drug pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjes su sngon sangs rgyas kyis spyad pa'i sems su
13a5(phal chen): lus kyi las dang / ngag gi las dang / yid kyi las kyis slob cing nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi spyod pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongs su bsngo ba med pas/ bla med pa yang
13a6(phal chen): dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bdun pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i sems rnam par dag cing 'od gsal ba dang khams
13a7(phal chen): cad du snang zhing kun tu 'od 'byung ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la snang zhing thams cad du snyoms pas/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongs su rdzogs par byed pa 'di ni ses
13a8(phal chen): gtso bo'i chos brgyad pa'o// 'jig rten pa'i 'deb thams cad yongs su spangs te/ 'jig rten pa'i dga' ba thams cad pa ma chags pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis
13b1(phal chen): gos pa med pa'i snod lam thams cad du mnyam pa nyid kyis/ 'jig rten thams cad bde ba thams cad dang ldan par byas te/ sdug bsngal dang spros pa thams cad rab tu 'joms pa 'di
13b2(phal chen): sems cad kyi gtso ba 'phos dag pa'o// sdug bsngal gyi mi bde bathams cad nyams su byab ste/ bgro ba thams cad kyi don du dka' thob gyis shin tu gdungs kyang shA bar sems bskyed
13b3(phal chen): pas/ sangs rgyas thams cad pa rags kyings su spang ba dang ldan pa dang / stobs bcu'i bar du sangs rgyas kyi yul la mos pas mthar thug pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos
13b4(phal chen): bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan
13b5(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du
13b6(phal chen): shegs pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad na bzhugs pa mi mnga' bar rnam
13b7(phal chen): spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na bzhugs pa dang bzhengs pa dang / bzhud pa chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par sbed pa
13b8(phal chen): yin no sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du chos ston pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
14a1(phal chen): 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas
14a2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad ni sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba'i mtha' la chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ 
14a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad tsam gyi 'khor kyi dkyil 'khor na bzugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas ba
14a4(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa la gzigs shing / thugs kyi skad gcig cig la chos 'grub chen po gsum gyis sems can rnam pa
14a5(phal chen): 'dul yang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gcig gis kyang tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam
14a6(phal chen): bar spyod pa chen por rnam par spyod kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams 'byam klas bya ma lus pa
14a7(phal chen): mas cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thug pa bsam gyis mi khyab par ston cing gsung yang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin te/ 
14a8(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dkon sangs rgyas
14b1(phal chen): com ldan 'das rnams kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla med pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku mtshan dang dpe byed padang po skye tshogs kyis nam
14b2(phal chen): par brgyan pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs kyis bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yan lag gi mchog dam pa drug
14b3(phal chen): dang ldan zhing yan lags brgyas yongs su bzung ba dang / rgyan brgya stong du mas rab tu 'argyan pa dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag mtha' las su med pas rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi
14b4(phal chen): chos kyi don dang tshig dang yi ge brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pas rab tu tshim par mdzad pa dang / bag tshab mi mnga' bar seng ge'i nga ro chen po sgrogs pa dang / 'jigs pa med pa chen
14b5(phal chen): 'os bsnyengs pa mi mnga' ra gyur pa dang / chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad sems can thams cad la grag cing stsal te/ khong du chud par 'gyur ba dang / sems can bsam pa
14b6(phal chen): tha dad pa dang / dbang po tha dad pa rnam pa sna tshogs 'dul bar nye bar gnas pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung gi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas
14b7(phal chen): ma ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi smin pas ni stobs bcus brgyan pa sangs rgyas kyi ting nge 'dzin chen po thams cad kyi me tog shin tu rgyas pa sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa
14b8(phal chen): 'i spyod yul dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi la rab tu rten pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos gting med pa rab
15a1(phal chen): / brnyes pa/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi rgyan du gyur pa/ dus gsum gyi chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can kun gyi sems dang spyod pa
15a2(phal chen): rnams cad skad cig gcig dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyis rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas
15a3(phal chen): com ldan 'das rnams ni 'od zer bye ba brjod du med pa rab tu 'gyed par mdzad de/ 'od zer de dag re re la yang 'od zer gyi 'khor gyi dra ba brjod du med pa dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi
15a4(phal chen): ning 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par snang bar byed cing 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad mun pa med par ston pa/ sangs rgyas skye ba dang mi 'bral bas/ sangs rgyas kyi
15a5(phal chen): da las las phyir mi ldog cing don yod pa/ sangs rgyas sto ba brjod du med pas gnas pa med pa rang bzhin rnam par dag cing kun tu snyoms par 'byung ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
15a6(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi 'od zer gyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams bzhad mo 'dzum par ston na/ zhal gyi sgo nas 'od zer kha dog sna tshogs
15a7(phal chen): dum dang ldan pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad snang bar byed pa sems can gyi khams tshad med grangs med
15a8(phal chen): mi 'ab pa rnam par ston pa/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar lung stong pa/ 'gro ba thams cad du shin tu gsal bar 'byung ste/ 
15b1(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis zhal 'dzum pa bstan pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku ni tshad med pa ste/ sgrib
15b2(phal chen): med pas rnam par dag pa chos thams cad la chags pa med pa nyid kyis mthar thug pa mtha' dang dbus med pa'i chos kyi dbyings la gnas pa/ 'jig rten thams cad dang ma 'dres pa 'ji
15b3(phal chen): thams cad dang 'dre ba med pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi de kho na nyid la yang dag par zhugs pa/ 'jig rten thams cad las gyen du 'phags pa/ 'jig rten thams cad las 'das
15b4(phal chen): pa'i chos kyis yang dag par spyod pa/ tshig gi lam dang bral ba/ brjod du med pa'i mthar phyin pa/ phung po dang khams dang / skye mched bral ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
15b5(phal chen): rnams kyi chos kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od tshad med pa mnga' ba ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du'ang nga
15b6(phal chen): 'dres shing / rgyun du ma dang ldan pa kha dog sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa'i 'od kyi snang ba kun tu thogs pa med cing / thams cad du chags pa med
15b7(phal chen): pa'od kyi dkyil 'khor sgrib pa med pa tshad med pa'i mdzod du gyur pa/ 'od thams cad kyi 'byung gnas su gyur pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rgyan mchog dam pa
15b8(phal chen): dmed pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni kha dege mtha' yas pa mnga' ba ste/ kha dog yid du 'ong ba mnga' ba'o// kha dog 'od gsal ba mnga' ba'o// kha dog tshad med pa mnga' 'a
16a1(phal chen): ma kyi mas rnams partsam bams bdag kyis pa bzhin dunam bya dmyigs pa'i bdin sa la ba'o// dem men pa ga
16a2(phal chen): khams gsum du gtogs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o// 'dog thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
16a3(phal chen): dog bran med pa mnga' ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi kha dog gan nA mchog dam pa zla med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge bas shin
16a4(phal chen): rnam par dag pa ste/ 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs dge ba rin po che'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa la shin tu byung ba'o// chos nyid
16a5(phal chen): rnam pa thams cad du khyad par yod pa dang khyad par med pa'i smod pas rnam par dag pa'i rgyan gyi ye shes skye ba thams cad kyi nang du gtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rig
16a6(phal chen): sgrib pa med pa'i rgyud rnam par dge bas/ 'jig rkyen gyi mi sbyin pa thams cad kyis ma sbyin par brjod du med pa rtse/ 'dri ni sangs rgyas macom ldan 'das rnams kyi sa ngas
16a7(phal chen): sa kyi rigs dang / rgyud rnam par dag pa'i rgyun mchog dam pa bla med pa'o// sangs chas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byams pa chen po'i mthu dang rang bzhin gyi rgyun mnga'
16a8(phal chen): ste/ shin tu dang bas yongs su rtog pa'i rtog pa mi mnga' ba sku'i phrin las yongs su bsal ba lta bas mi skyo ba/ dgengs pa shin tu rnam par bsal ba thugs rje chen po
16b1(phal chen): 23/ 'gro ba thams cad skyob pa yon tan gyi gnas kyi dam pa bla na med pa yongs su 'dzin pa'i nang na thugs brtse ba can phan par mdzad pa sems can thams cad kyi don tu tshwa
16b2(phal chen): shes chen po byin gyis brlabs te/ bsod nams chen pos yongs su 'phags pa 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing du gyur pa sems can rnams kyi yon tan dang / ye
16b3(phal chen): shes phung po thams cad rnam par 'phel bar mdzad pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byams pa chen po dang / sngags rje chen po'i mthar thug pa'i bsod nams
16b4(phal chen): tan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras
16b5(phal chen): bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bskur ba'i chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
16b6(phal chen): chos thams cad la mnga' ba dang / chos thams cad snang bar mdzad pa'i mnga' bskur bas/ tshig dang yi ge mtha' yas pa la thogs pa mi mnga' ba'i spobs pa mnga' ba dang / 
16b7(phal chen): thams cad ma lus par yongs su brjod pas mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos dang blo'o// 
16b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can ji ltar yongs su smin pa dang / smon lam ji ltar btab pa'i tshul bzhin du/ 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' bas mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni
17a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos gnyis pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad sems
17a2(phal chen): can gcig la yang gnod pa med par nam pa drug du rab tu bskyod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams can rnam par bkod pa grangs med tshad med pa dang ldan pa nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthus
17a3(phal chen): gtugs pa thams cad gcig nas gcig tu 'phang ba dang / gcig nas gcig tu bzhug pa dang / gcig nas gcig tu bsdu ba dang / gcig nas gcig tu bsrabs 'jig rten gyi
17a4(phal chen): khams gzhan dang gzhan dag gzhan gyi phyogs su rab tu bzhag kyang sems can gyi khams rnams 'khor zhing mongs par mi 'gyur la/ the tsom du mi 'gyur bar mdzad pas mnga'
17a5(phal chen): nisangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos gsum pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad byin gyis
17a6(phal chen): brlob pa'i ye shes kyis 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyan phan tshun du byin gyis brlab pa dang / dgongs pa'i skad cig gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rgyan yang dag par bstan// 
17a7(phal chen): pa dang / bskal pa grangs med par brjod kyang yi ge shin tu bstan pa zad mi shes pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rgyan thams cad kyis rnam par brgyan
17a8(phal chen): pa dang / mi mthun pa med cing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig tu yongs su 'du bar sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa thams cad byin gyis
17b1(phal chen): 'drabs pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mda' bsgyur ba'i chos bzhipa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
17b2(phal chen): ni sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i sems can gzigs na sems can gcig gi don du bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par skyil mo krung gcig gis bzhugs na yang de
17b3(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la mi bde ba mi mnga' zhing thugs la mi bde ba mi mnga' ste/ gang zag de yang mi skyel bas 'dul ba'i dus las mi 'da' ba dang / gang zag gcig la ji lta
17b4(phal chen): ba de bzhin du rim pa rim pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du phyi ma'i mtha' mur thug pa'i sku tshe la mnga' bar byin gyis brlab te bzhugs kyang / 
17b5(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams la skyob mi mnga' ste/ 'di ltar sems can gyi khams thams cad mthar gyis rim pas sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i gang zag gi don du yongs su bskyod
17b6(phal chen): par mdzad pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos lnga pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig
17b7(phal chen): rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du yang dag par gzhol ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i bzhud pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du bzhud pa la thag thogs mi mnga' ba dang / 
17b8(phal chen): gas bcu'i chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi chud rgya mtsho 'byam klas pa dang / phyogs kyi dra ba'i rgyud thams cad du dgongs pa'i skad cig
18a1(phal chen): gcig dang thun pa'i bzhud par byin gyis brlob cing / chos kyi dbyings shin tu bathun pa khong du chud par bya bas chos kyi 'khor lo thogs pa ma
18a2(phal chen): bArab tu bskyor ba la ma 'chem ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ma mchen pos mnga' bster sa rdzog pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ra
18a3(phal chen): ni 'dul ba'i sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi don du dgongs pa'i skad cig re re la/ blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bar mnga' cheb ste// 
18a4(phal chen): de la chos thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas pa gang yang med la/ gang mngon par sangs rgyas pa gang yang med la/ gang gis mngon par sangs rgyas pa'ang med de/ mngon
18a5(phal chen): ra 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ba med kyang slob pa'i sa la gnas shing / mngon par 'tshang rgya bar yang mi brjod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang sgrib pa med par rtogs pa
18a6(phal chen): thugs su chud pas/ sems can thams cad gdul ba'i don du ye shes tshad med pa'i tshul gyis sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chen po'i yul yongs su rgyun me gtsad pa
18a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos bdun pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni spyan gyi skye
18a8(phal chen): sakyi phrin las gang bslab pa de snyan gyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do// snyan gyi skye mched kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de shangs kyi skye mched kyis
18b1(phal chen): yongs su grub par mdzad do// shangs kyi bye bached swa sangs rgyas kyi phyin las gang bsgrub pa de sngags kyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do// sngags kyi skye mtsha
18b2(phal chen): kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de ni sku'i skye mched kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do// sku'i skye mched kyis sangs kyis kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de thugs kyi skye mtsha
18b3(phal chen): kyis yongs su grub par mdzad do// thugs kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub pa de 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi dmigs pa 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig
18b4(phal chen): las 'das pa sna tshogs rnam par phye ba thams cad grub par mdzad do// de bzhin du dmigs pa thams cad re re yang snrel la nir bsgrub pas sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsgrub pa la ma pa
18b5(phal chen): ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mngar bsgyur ba'i chos brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rang gi sku'i ba spu'i bu ga gcig gi
18b6(phal chen): du sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad gzung ba mdzad cing khongs su chud par mdzad pa dang / sems can re re zhing yang lus sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa tsam du yangs par
18b7(phal chen): dzad kyang sems can de dag la gnod par mi 'gyur ba dang / de dag du yang sems can re re zhing 'jig rten gyi khams gcig tu brgyud pas bskal pa grangs med pa zad par gnas par
18b8(phal chen): bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med par zhim pa gcig gis phyin pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag du sangs rgyas byung ba rnams kyi spyan sngar 'gro bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas ded
19a1(phal chen): byung ba'i tshe yang brjod du med pa'i 'jig rten gyis khams kyi rgyud dang / gling de dag na sems can gyi gtso bo brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i chos
19a2(phal chen): 'khor lo bskor bar bya ba dang / ba spu'i bu ga de nas sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pas brjod du med pa'i yang 'dzad du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang / sems canag rjeg nas
19a3(phal chen): gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo gci gnas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa'i lang brjod du med pa bskor bar bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings bsta
19a4(phal chen): pa gcig nas gcig tu chud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin tu bstan par bya ba dang / 'das pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa dang / ma 'ongs pa
19a5(phal chen): gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa dang / da ltar byung ba gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa yongs su brjod par bya ba dang / dam mkha'i dbyings mtha' dang dbus
19a6(phal chen): med par bstan pa kun tu mtshams ba par sems can thams cad 'ong zhing 'gro ba dang / skye ba'i skye ma ched thams cad du 'dod pa'i longs spyad rgya chen po gegs med pa thams cad
19a7(phal chen): 'byung bar bya ba la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mang 'brasbyar ba'i chos dgu pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
19a8(phal chen): rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad pad mos brgyan pa'i seng ge'i khri pad mo'i snying po can la de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi chos kyang
19b1(phal chen): pa'i skus byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongs su bstan par mdzad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gis ji lu ba
19b2(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams sems can gyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi sems can gyi gcod mams cad kyang de bzhin du dgongs pa skad cig ma re re'i byin gyi rlabs kyis brlab pa dang / dgongs
19b3(phal chen): skad cig la ji lta ba de bzhin du dgongs pa skad cig ma thams cad la yang / pad mo'i rgyud kyis yongs su dag par mngon par 'tshang rgya bar bya ba dang / de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings tham
19b4(phal chen): dam lus pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa rnam par dag pa/ rgyan sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams su dmigs pa rnam pa sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i zhing rnam par dag pa
19b5(phal chen): 'byam klas pa/ brjod du med pa mtshan nyid tha dad pa rnam pa tha dad pa'i rgyud tshad med cing 'byam klas pa/ dus kyi rgyud grangs med pa dang ldan pa bstan pa ma 'dres pa dang ldan pa/ blo tshad med pa
19b6(phal chen): mos pa shin tu yangs pa dang ldan pa/ mtshan nyid sna tshogs kyi gnas med pa/ mtshan nyid bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa/ tshad med pa thams cad dgongs pa skad cig ma las dgongs pas
19b7(phal chen): cig ma gcig gis thams cad yongs su bstan kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ched du bslab pa'i mdzad pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
19b8(phal chen): ngas rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba'i chos bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag gis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' bsgyur ba
20a1(phal chen): chos so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa tshad med pa bsam gyi mi khyab pa rnams te/ 
20a2(phal chen): bcu gang zhe na/ mtshan re re zhing bsod nams brgya ba'i mtshan yongs su dag par 'gyur ba 'ang ni yongasu rdzogs pa dang po ste/ des sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon
20a3(phal chen): par 'tshang rgya'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams yongs su rdzogs pas/ sangs rgyas co ldan 'das da chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya 'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzos
20a4(phal chen): pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// yon tan thams cad kyi 'byung gnas phun sum tshogs pa'i spyod pa yongs su dag pa yongs su rdzogs
20a5(phal chen): pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// sems can yongs su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
20a6(phal chen): mas byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// sangs rgyas kyi mnga' 'gro ba thams cad kyis zil gyi mi non pa/ yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byung chub
20a7(phal chen): ngon par 'chang rgya'o// zhing yongs su dag par bya ba yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i se
20a8(phal chen): com ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang bya'o// mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang gzugs kyi
20b1(phal chen): bas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldar
20b2(phal chen): 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ste/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las yongs su rdzogs par mdzad nas yongs su mya ngan las 'dra'o// rgyal ba'i sras bcu po dag ni sangs
20b3(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
20b4(phal chen): rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos thams cad byin gyis brlabs pa med cing spros pa thams cad med par yang thugs su
20b5(phal chen): tud la/ dge ba'i sgo nas sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyang shin tu ston cing brjod de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa dang
20b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la gzigs pa med cing phan tshun du mkhyen pa med do// ma bcings ma grol ba dang gzung ba med cing bsags pa med do// 
20b7(phal chen): yongs su rdzogs pa med par yang thugs su chud la sangs rgyas kyis chos thams cad la mnga' dam pa'ang brnyes te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos thams cad la ma
20b8(phal chen): sbyar ba de yang / yang dag pa de kho na nyid pa nor ba rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur ba dang / chos thams cad ngadag gi med
21a1(phal chen): / yang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na mnga' chen pos chos kyi dbyings thams cad snang ba la yang / rab tur khyen pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
21a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa gnyis pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mtshan ma'i mtha' thams cad mi mnga' ste/ mtshan ma thams cad dang mi 'grogs shang / mtshan ma
21a3(phal chen): mngon par shes pa thams cad dang ma 'dres la de'i rang bzhin du ngo bo nyid med pa dang / ji ltar ngo bo nyid med pa'i sgra'i tshul thams cad thugs su chud pas kyang gzugs kyi mtshan ma'i sdug
21a4(phal chen): rngab par dag pa grangs med pa dang / zheng gi mtshan ma dang rnam par spyod pa'i mtshan ma zad mi shes pa rnam pa sna tshogs yang dag par bstan cing bshad pa'i ye shes kyi phung po mun pa med pa
21a5(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad kyi sgron ma chen po dgyur pas mun pa med pa'i snong ba stod pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan radas rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa gsum pa'o// chags pa ma
21a6(phal chen): tha' ni sngon gyi mtha' yang ma yin/ phyi ma'i mtha' yang ma yin/ de ltar byung ba yang ma yin te/ chos kyi dbyings su gnas pa ni 'das pa 'am/ ma 'ongs pa dang / da spar byung ba yang ma yin pa
21a7(phal chen): de bzhin nyid kyis mtshan nyid kyis 'byung ba med kyang / sangs rgyas 'byung ba rnams kyi rigs tshad med pa'i phyir shin tu bstan pa brjod du med pas 'das pa dang / 
21a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas skye ba yang rab tu 'arjod cing kun 'gazigs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis de bzhin du gzigs pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs ma khas
21b1(phal chen): bzhi pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni spyi'i phrin las dang gsung gi phrin las dang / thugs kyi sprin las kyis mngon par 'du mdzad pa yang mi mnga' la/ yongs su blang ba mi mnga' ba
21b2(phal chen): bzhugs shing / rnam par phye ba med pa'i mthar thug pa ste/ dor ba med pa'i chos kyi gnas kyi pha rol tukhyen pa la kha grang ba'i tshul las rnam par 'das kyang tshul nges pa med pa'i mdod du rgyu
21b3(phal chen): / bgrang dang mngon par bsgrub pa mtha' yas pa dang / 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa rnam pa sna tshogs tha dad pa'i grangs kyi rdul thugs su chud pa ye shes sgrib pa med
21b4(phal chen): gzigs pa rnams te/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can gdul ba rnam par dmigs pa la/ rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs tshad med mu med par mngon par bsgrub pa
21b5(phal chen): mdzad pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa lnga pa'o// chos thams cad lta ba med pas tha mi dad pa dang bye brag med pa dang / 'byung ba med pa dang ma
21b6(phal chen): nyid med pa dang / sna tshogs med pa dang / blang ba med pa dang / dor ba med pa dang / rang bsnyen med par rab tu mkhyen kyang / chos kyi rgyur shir rta nges pa yang dag par bsku
21b7(phal chen): cing 'jig rten gyi tshul dang 'gal ba med pa dang / rang bzhin med pa yang dag par gzigs pas thams cad mkhyen pa/ thams cad gzigs pa/ mkhyen par bya ba
21b8(phal chen): cad ma lus par gzigs par chos la mnga' bsgyur ba thams cad kyang rab tu ston lanade bzhin nyid kyi rang bzhin las kyang mi nyams pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
22a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'dris ni thugs su chud pa'i rnam pa gcig gis gzhan dang gnan mkhyen par bya ba cho/ 
22a2(phal chen): de'i skyon med pa las rnam par ma 'das pa gnas med pa dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par dag pa mnyam pa med kyi chos sbyin med pas/ dus thams cad du gnas pa
22a3(phal chen): gcig gam/ zla 'a byed dam/ lo gcig gam/ la brgya'am/ bskal pa gcig pa dang / 'du bas rjes su bsgag pa dang / phyir phyogs pa mi mnga' bar du sa tshad med pa dang / nyi ma gcig dang / 
22a4(phal chen): datsam gcig gi dus dang sa dro nas nyi ma byed kyi dus dang / phyi dro nas snga dro'i dus dang / nyi mgung nas phyi dro'i dus dang / nyam bgrangs pa'i dus dang / nyi ma bdun dang / zla ba phyed kyi dus
22a5(phal chen): dang / zla ba dang / lo dang / lo brgya'i dus dang bskal pa gcig gi dus dang / tshad med grangs med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dus nas/ phyi ma'i mtho de lung thug pa'i dus su chos bstan pa dang / 
22a6(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor mo thogs pa med cing phyir mi ldog/ na d+ha bar mi 'gyur/ bral bar mi 'gyur/ ba chad par mi 'gyur/ med pa ma 'gyur/ 'jig pa 'gyur gamo bar mi byu gari du mi gyu
22a7(phal chen): de la gnas pa nyid du yang rgyun chad par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bdur pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na
22a8(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings pa lus pa sems cad du cag tu dus ya ba par bzhugs pa ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi 'jigs pa tshad med pa mnga' ba'o// so so yang dag par rig pa
22b1(phal chen): grangs med pa mang 'a ba'o// sos yang dag par dag 'tshad med par bar ba'o// sa so yang dag par rig pa rad mi gle yang ba'o// so yang dag par rig moslo pa med pa mang ra / sas yang dag par dag pa mtha' chub ma
22b2(phal chen): thun mong ma yin pa'i seMs yang dag par rig pa mnga' ba'o// so so yang dag par rig pa mthar thug pa med pa mnga' ba'o// so so yang dag par rig pa de yon dang ldan pa mnga' ba'o// so so yang
22b3(phal chen): dag par rig pa TIg gi tshul thams cad rab tu rtogs pa mang ba'o// che thams cad som yang dag par rig pa mnga' ba'o// bsam pa dang mos pad dbang po nges pa bzhin du chos kyi tsulang
22b4(phal chen): nam grangs tshul ji ltar rnam par bkod pa bzhin dus 'tshams med par ston te/ mdo sde bye ba khrag khrig brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa rnams mdo sde dang de la thog ma dang dbus kyi tshul gyi
22b5(phal chen): yang dag par ston to// 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni ming med kyang ming dang rigs su byung
22b6(phal chen): ba'i chos thams cad mig dang yi ges shin tu sbyangs pa'i dbyangs mngon par sangs rgyas pa ste/ ming 'das pa ma yin pa dang / ming ma 'ongs pam yin pa dang / mad da ltar byung gA ma yin pa dang / ma
22b7(phal chen): sems can ma yin pa dang / ming zhing ma yin pa dang / ming chos ma yin pa dang ming yon tan ma yin pa dang / med byang chub sems dpa' ma yin pa dang / ming sangs rgyas ma yin pa dang / ming grang
22b8(phal chen): ma yin pa dang / med grangs med pa ma yin pa dang / ming skye ba ma yin pa dang / ming 'gag pa ma yin pa dang / ying med pa ma yin pa dang / ming yod pa ma yin pa dang / meng gcig pa ma len pa da
23a1(phal chen): meng ba dad pa ma yin pa dang / ming thams cad ma yin pa dang / chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis brjod du med pa dang / phyogs med pa dang brda med pa dang / tshig ga lam med
23a2(phal chen): pasgra dang bral ba dang / skra'i rnam pa thams cad mi 'byung ba/ yongs su bsgrub pa med pa/ byas pa dang rnam par byas pa med pa rnam pa gcig ma yin pa/ rnam pabang po ma yin pa yang thugs
23a3(phal chen): chud la/ brjod pa dang skyed pa thams cad la yang pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog po rnyes pa dag ste/ rnam par rtog pa'i yul mi mnga' ba drug go// mngon par 'du mdzad pa med pa la rab tu brtson pa
23a4(phal chen): sogs pa dang kun tu rtog pa yang yongs su rtog pa 'gags bdag go// spyod pa thams cad la mi gnas par spyod pa dag ste// 'don sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs
23a5(phal chen): thabs labs pa dgu pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad kyi gzugs ma skyes pa rabs mkhyen pa tshor pa'i spros pa med pa dang / 'du shes kyi grangs med
23a6(phal chen): 'du byed kun tu sgrub med pa dang / rnam par shes pa nye bar len pa med pa dang / rang ba zhin gyis ni b.rab tu mkhyen te/ chos thams cad skye ma tshad kyi rgyud med pa dang / khams rnams med kyi
23a7(phal chen): pa dang / chos thams cad mi 'jigs pa dang / chos thams cad bskyed du med cing / rang bzhin gyis nam mkha' lwa bu dang / chos thams cad dben pa dang / las med pa dang / rnam par smid pa/ 
23a8(phal chen): dpa dang / spyod pas 'byung ba med pa dang / ma gakha pa dang / mabyung ba dang / grangs kyis ma brjod pa dang / yod pa ma yin pa dang / med pa ma yin pa dang / ma skyes pa dang ma 'gags pa dang / 
23b1(phal chen): dam nyan mongs pa med pa dang / rnam par byang ba med pa dang / bya ba med pa dang gnas pa med pa dang / yongs su gnas pa med pa dang / yongs su smin par byas pa dang / rnam par gtum pa med pa dang / 
23b2(phal chen): mas can med pa dang / sems can mod pa mayin pa dang / srog med pa dang / srog med pam yin pa dang / rkyen med pa dang / rkyen med pa ma yin pa dang / rkyen med pa dang / rkyen med pa ma yin
23b3(phal chen): chos thams ca dbugs su chud kyang chos kyi dbyings thams cad shin tu bstan pa la pha rol tu phyin pa'i dram pa brnyes bdag ste/ nges pa dang pa nges pa dang / log par nges pa'i phung po gsum
23b4(phal chen): rnam par dgod pa rnamapa la skabs bcu ga thugs ma chud pa'i ma 'jigs pa bzhis rnam par dag pa'i sangs rgyas kyi lnga la chen po dang ldan pas seng ge'i sgra sgrog pa 'di na sangs rgyas
23b5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu pa de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa'o// // shin tu rgyas pa
23b6(phal chen): chen po'i mdo sangs rgyas mdag cad ces bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo// bam po gsum pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dka ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnas kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las rgya chen po tshad me
23b7(phal chen): papasaM gyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ de dag spangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs ma gtogs par lha dang bzlas pa'i 'jig nyen dang / 'das pa dang / mA 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nyan pos dang / rang
23b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas thams cad kyis 'jug pa mi nus pa'o// bcu gang zhe na/ phyogs bcu'i dam mkha'i dbyings kyi mazas gtugs pa'i chos kyi dbyings thams cad 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus
24a1(phal chen): / khazas cad du dga' ldan du skye ba bstan pa dang / byang ba sem pa pa'i spyod pa su med pa dag la sangs chus kyi phrin las mdzad de// ba dag chad med pa gce rjidu cad med pa snang ba
24a2(phal chen): med pa/ dbyangs tshad med pa dbyangs kyi yad lal rnam par dag pa cad med pa gsung brjod pas rnam par dmigs pa tshad me pa/ ting nge 'dzim cad med pa la spyod pa/ shes rab dang ye shes
24a3(phal chen): kyi yum tshad med pa mnga' ba rnams lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de/ bdud dang bcas pa tshangs pa dang bcas pa/ dge sbyong dang bcas po// bram ze'i skye dgu dang brtsa
24a4(phal chen): bskra dang me dang/ lha ba yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// byams pa chen po'i spyod chul thogs pa med pa dang / thab 'thogs de chen po'i sgo'i mthar thug pas
24a5(phal chen): can la yad 'dogs pa mdzad do// bsod nams kyi stobs dang / mnga' phun sum tshogs pa dang / dbang po rnam par sbyangs pa dang / cang shes kyi sems yongs su dag pas kyang sems
24a6(phal chen): nams la phan 'dogs par med do// thegapa chags rnam par dag pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa med do// reg pa chen po yongs su rdzogs par bya bas kyang sems
24a7(phal chen): na rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// 'gro ba thams cad gnod pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi
24a8(phal chen): de las dang po'o// dga' ldaran gyi pho brang nas 'phos pa med kyang yul gyi skur gshegs shing / byang chub sems dpa'i sgrub ma skye bar ston la sgyum du/ pur yongs su spyod pa/ smras
24b1(phal chen): ting nge 'dzin rje mthar thug pa/ mig yong/ khur rnam par dmigs pa/ na 'i yus chad me par khyab pa/ bzhed pa pan du skye ba yang chags pa mi mnga' bru/ sreg sgyulta zur bstan pa/ 
24b2(phal chen): mongs pa med pa'i chos la yang dag par gzhal ba/ gnas med pa'i me thes la gnas pa/ rang bzhin gyis 'dod pan pa dang brim gson ma par dag pa/ rgyan shin che ba'i mdzod kyis sa
24b3(phal chen): rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// khang pa brtsegs pa rin po che las byas pa'i pho brang chen po rin po che'i rgya mang po dang ldan pa na bzhugs pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// 
24b4(phal chen): rdzu 'phrul gyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// yid la bya ba'i byin gyi brlabs chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// rnam par 'phrul pa'i mdzod chen po yang dag par/ 
24b5(phal chen): bstan pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// ye shes kyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// mus sku bskyed pa'i spyan bzhugs pas kyangs
24b6(phal chen): rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi spyod yul chen po badres pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi srin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis 'jig tIn byin gyis brlabs pa
24b7(phal chen): tha' yas pas sangs rgyas kyi phrin lngas mdzad do// ting nge 'dzin ched po grangs med pa la rnam par spyad cing / snyoms par 'jug pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin lngas mdzad do// ting
24b8(phal chen): dzidzin las bzhengs pa de dang de dag gis kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// spyod pa'i thog ma la yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po'i mthar thug pa'i bar du thogs pa
25a1(phal chen): dbus dang tha ma'i tshul gyis sangs rgyas kyi 'phrin las mdzad do// sa 'di la gnyis su med pas thams cad mthar phyin par byas nas tha mar 'jig rten gyi grangs
25a2(phal chen): skyeb yang san // myangs kyang 'deg rten thams saca dang sangs kyis na dus/ na dung gyu pas kyang 'dre/ rkyen pams med dus rgyas kyi phrin pa meng da/ 
25a3(phal chen): rgab sems dpang gyur pas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las ma de de// mngon par 'byung bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do/ 
25a4(phal chen): da par 'chang rgyabs kyang 'jig rten pa med chad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las medzad do// chos kyi 'khor la bskor bas kyang 'jig can thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mang da
25a5(phal chen): thabs mkhas pa sna tshogs kyis kyang 'jig rten sna tshogs 'jig rten tshad med pa/ 'jig rten kun tu mtha' las pa phyogs kyi dra ba'i rgyud dang / dus thams cad ci 'jig rten ma lus

25a8(phal chen): las mdzad do// sprul pa chen po'i rgyud dang / sangs cas kyi rigs dang / ches dran pa'i sgo'i 'khor los kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom

26a1(phal chen): la rtog par bya ba mdzad cing spong ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa bas rnam par skyed pa yang dag par bstan pa dang / ji ltar bkod pa'i tshul du sems can gdul ba dang /

26a4(phal chen): bdang / thugs rje chen po las byung ba chos kyi sprin gyis mngon par skyeng bdang / thams cad la skyob pa 'byams pa chen po bskyed pa'i cho 'phrul gsum byas yo rlan pa dang / sa

26a8(phal chen): na las kyi mtha' zab cing chags pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i thabs la mkhas pas sems cad rnams kyi don mdzad de 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas
26b1(phal chen): kyi phrin las gsum pa'o// rnam par rgyal ba chen po mnga' ba rnams ni btsun mo'i 'khor rgyan rnam par phye 'a tshad med pa dang ldan pa yid du 'ong ba spangs te/ mngon par 'byung ba'i/

26b4(phal chen): mongs pa byang zhing nub pa la yang dag par spyod par bya ba dang / sems can gyi don rjes su dran par bya ba'i phyir/ mngon par 'byung ba'i don la rab tu gzhol ba dang / khyim pa'i tshul

26b6(phal chen): med pa yongs su sdang bar bya ba dang / ye shes kyi dkyil lo khor chen po brnyes pas sems can rnams kyi ye shes pa'i sgrib pa rab tu bsal ba dang / bdag nyid bsod nams kye ning
26b7(phal chen): na med par gyur par 'gro ba thams cad la bstan pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i nang du 'dus par 'gro ba thams cad la yang drag
26b8(phal chen): brjod pa dang / bdag nyid kyis ye shes kyi don gzigs par bstan pa dang / sems can rnams rnam par dag pa'i sgor brjod pa dang / sems can rnams khar mtho ba med pa'i
27a1(phal chen): bsgrub pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad du 'byung ba'i sgo rab tu bstan pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rgyal mtshan yang dag par bsgred pas mdzad cing
27a2(phal chen): mdod par 'byung ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi phrin las ban pa 'o// don gcig mo yod pa mkhyen pa dang ldan pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi mtha
27a3(phal chen): thag pa ma sa ni chos thams cad mngon par 'chang skye bar bya'o zhes byang chub kyi shing drung du byon te/ byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bas kyang bdud kyi da zung thams cad rab tu
27a4(phal chen): gnom pa dang / sgra'i byin gyi brlabs kyi mdzod kyi tshal kyi dbyid sa kyi ma lus pa thams myed dus su myur drug ba'i phyid byin gyis rlabs 'dam ge khyi ma par thug pas mar
27a5(phal chen): dam byar spangs pa spyod pa cad med pa rab tu brjes pa thams cad mabyon pa'i pham kyis rnam par ma po ye shes kyi don dang ldan pa/ rnams cad mkhyed pa'i yon tan yang dag par ba
27a6(phal chen): pa yongs su rdzogs pa 'jig rten gyis khams ma lus pa thams cad du gdan rnam par bkram pas yongs su rgyas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi ning ma lus pa thams cad du byang chub sems dpas
27a7(phal chen): ma par dmigs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dam pathob pa rnams kyi zhal du blta ba/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi rnam pa dang / smon lam khyad par can dang ldan pa'i byang chub
27b1(phal chen): sems dpa' brjod du med pa'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa sna tshogs spyod pa la yang dag par gnol ba/ byang chub sems dpa' 'a'ang kyi dkyil 'khor nam
27b2(phal chen): par dag pa mnga' ba 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis byin du brlob pa'i yul yang 'gu dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa'i sems can gyis rnam par dmigs pa/ dge ba
27b3(phal chen): rtsa ba thams cad tha me dad pa dang ldan pa 'byung ba'i sa/ byang chub sems drapa'i spyod pa mtha' yas pa'i mthu'i gnas la yon tan gyis khyad par thams cad rab tu brnyes nas bzhugs pa/ 
27b4(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi rnam pa thams cad me lus po'i mthar thug pa/ sems cad gyi rnam pa thams cad dang / zhing gi rnam pa thams cad dang / chos kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'
27b5(phal chen): rnam pa thams cad dang / yongs su smin par bya ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang / dus kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / gdul ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul ba'i rnam
27b6(phal chen): thams cad ma lus pa'i mthar thug pa rnams 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad du mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par 'tshang rgyabs sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
27b7(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las lnga pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba mdzad pa'i phyir mi ldog pa'i tshul gyis phyir mi ldog pa'i la
27b8(phal chen): lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyi khong du chud par 'gyur ba'i tshul gyis tshad med pa'i 'khor lo dang / mi 'jigs pa'i seng ge'i nga ro chen po'i tshul gyis thams cad ma lus par mngon pa
28a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas pa'i 'khor lo dang / gos kyi mdzod su med pa'i sgos snang bar byed pa'i tshul gyi chos thams cad 'khyen pa'i mdzod kyi 'khor lo dang / ye shes nam mkha'/ 
28a2(phal chen): dbyings ltar tshad med pa'i tshul gyis chags pa med pa'i 'khor lo dang / mos mams cad kyi dngos po med pa'i rang bzhin rab tu rtogs par bya ba'i rgyal gyis sgrib pa med pa'i 'khor lo dang // 
28a3(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyi chos kyi mig rnam par sbyong ba'i tshul gyis 'jig rten thams cad kyi smon la re 'khor lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad du rgyas par 'grengs pa'i tshul gyis
28a4(phal chen): dmakhyen pa'i chos brjod pa'i 'khor lo dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dang mi 'gal ba'i tshul gyis sangs rgyas thams cad 'dab 'dres par gyur pa'i 'khor lo dang / de dag la
28a5(phal chen): sogs pa rnam pabye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas sems can 'ams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa'i rnam pa la/ chos kyi 'khor long bskor te/ de sur chos kyi 'khor
28a6(phal chen): lo bskor bas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad do// 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
28a7(phal chen): drug pa'o// sangs rgyas com ldan 'das rnams ni grong dang grong khyer dang grong dal dang / rgyal po'i gnas su gshegs pas kyang sems
