28b1(phal chen): lding gi rgyal po gnas dang / ma 'am n+da'i rgya mtha' gnas dang / nam bya chen mo gnas dang / phrin na rgyal ban sha ra'i rgyal po'i gnas dag tu gshegs pas kyang sangs rgyas
28b2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di lta ste/ grong khyer gyi sgor byon nas g.yo ba dang / 'od zer snang ba dang / long ba rnams mig 'thob pa dang / 'on pa rnams smra
28b3(phal chen): bar 'gyur ba dang / smyon pa rnams dran pa thob par 'gyur ba dang / gis med pa rnams gos thob par 'gyur ba dang / sdug bsngal ba rnams bde bathob pa dang / rom mo'i cha spyad pa dkrol ma 'ang
28b4(phal chen): bar sgrayid du 'ong ba nga 'byin pa dang / rgyan rjod na 'dug pa dang / gnas nas mthog pa dang / ma bskyod pa grol bar bskyod cing dkrol ba'i sgra 'byung ba dag byang rdzog sa mang ba'i sgra spang 'i
28b5(phal chen): 'ong ba 'byung ba dang / bstan gtang mi bri zhing mi 'thun pa med pa'i sku mthong bas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'drab rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// 
28b6(phal chen): dad dper byed pabang po bstan pas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'ad sngornams sems can rnams la sangs kyi gyi phrin las mdzad de/ mangs su gzigs pa dang / rnam par gzigs pa
28b7(phal chen): dang / brkyang ba dang / bskum pas kyang sems can rnams las nges rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// gshegs pa dang slar bzhud pa dang / bzhengs pa dang / 'dzag pa dang / bzhugs pa dang / gzims pa
28b8(phal chen): kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// chos bstan pa dang / mi gsung bar bzhugs pa la kyang sems cad rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phra las padzad do// rdzu 'phrul
29a1(phal chen): bzhugs pa dang / yongs su bzhugs pas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mir chad do// 'di ni sangs rgyas
29a2(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi phrin las brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rgyu pas la 'byung gnas l+h+wa bu// sems can thams cad kyi bsam
29a3(phal chen): kun la rnam par sbyong ba lta bu/ sangs rgyas rnams la dad pa lta bu/ sems khong du chud par bya ba la shin tu mos pa lta bu/ dbang po rnams la bsgrub pa lta bu/ sems can skye dgu
29a4(phal chen): cad la 'dul ba tshus/ 'gro ba rnams cad la mos pa lta bu/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la 'byung ba lta bu/ byang chub tu zhugs pa rnams mi bskul ba lta bu/ gzhan gyi drang
29a5(phal chen): 'jog pa rnams la ye shes kyi snang ba lta bu dag ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten mi rtag par ston pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad pa
29a6(phal chen): brjod pa dang / phrin las mdzad pa'i mthar thug par bstan pa dang / chos kyi rgyun tu nyams pa med pa'i dngos por brjod pa dang / srid pa'i tshul rtsabanas chad dper brjod pa dang / 
29a7(phal chen): canathaMdade skyob dbye bar bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi rjes su 'gro ba'i sems su mazhun par bya ba dang / sku tsha'i mtha' lte bur sems can+da rnams kyis shes par bya ba dang / sems
29a8(phal chen): can rnams kyis 'jig rten thams cad du dga' bar bya ba med par bstan pa dang / sems can rnams la ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas gcig nas/ gcig du brgyud pa mnyes par
29b1(phal chen): gyis shig par bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba bstan du mi rung bar khong du chud par bya ba dang / 'jig rten rnams kyi rtsol ba bskyed pa
29b2(phal chen): dang sangs rgyas la dmigs par brtson pa'i sems la dgod pa dang / yul tu dran pa rnam par dag pas de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba'i rnam par rtog/ bskyed pa dang / skye ba'i
29b3(phal chen): phyir bzlog cing yongs su dag par mdzad pa dang / sangs rgyas la mos pa bskyed pa dang / skyo bar gyur pa'i sems can rnams la byin gyis brlab par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas la dmigs
29b4(phal chen): pa'i rkyen 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du phyin par dgongs po mdzad pa dang / sku thams cad bshig ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung gis sems can rnams yongs
29b5(phal chen): sugazung ba mdzad pa dang / 'jig rten rnam par 'khrug pa dang / regs shing myos pa'i sems can rnams sdom pa la bkod pa mdzad cing / yongs su mya ngan las 'da' bstod pas kyang / 
29b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi phrin ma rgyun rje 'chad de/ 'di na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis ngas rgyas kyi phrin las dgu pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mya ngan las 'das pa'i tshe/ 'jig rten thams ca
29b7(phal chen): dasems can rnams smre sngags 'don cing ngu ba dang / mya ngan byed pa dang / 'arjem 'byin pa dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de 'am/ thugs rje chen ba zhe'am/ ded dpon chen// 
29b8(phal chen): na'am/ phan par bzhed pa zhugs brtse ba can ne las/ lnga dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi sems can thams cad kyi skyabs su gyur pa/ mgon du gyur pa/ rten du gyur pa/ rgyun
30a1(phal chen): 'phrul dang / yongs su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul dang / rjes su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul gyis kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul sems
30a2(phal chen): can bsam pa sna chags kyi mtsho dang ldan pa 'jig rten gyi spyod pa thams cad shing 'byung ba dang ldan pa dge pa'i rtsa badzin pas shin tu brtan pa/ sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa dang ldan gas
30a3(phal chen): 'grogs 'grogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' dang gnas pa'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams ni sku ga zugs
30a4(phal chen): bstan mi ngoms pa'o zhes bya bar gshel ba dang / sangs rgyas rnams skye bar dkon no zhes bya bar yid ches par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mthong zhing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i
30a5(phal chen): gsung thob pa ni bsod nams kyi chos dkar po'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa'o// zhes sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa yid la byed pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad rnam par dag pa ni/ de bzhin gshegs
30a6(phal chen): bskye ba yin no zhes bya bar khong du chud par byed pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi yon tan bsngags pa ni mtha' bas pa'o zhes bya bar yang dag par lta ba dang / ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas 'byung
30a7(phal chen): gshegs pa'i rigs yang dag par bslab pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba dang mos pa'i tshul thams cad kyis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mnyes par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs
30a8(phal chen): rnams ni yon tan mtha' yas pa'o nas khong du rma pa byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa de sems can thams cad mngon tu gyur par rtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni sems
30b1(phal chen): can gyi nges bsam gyis mi khyab par gnas su sbyar bar sems pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni 'ang thams cad na snang bar khong du chud pa dang / de lta bu'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad 'byung bas
30b2(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// dad par bya ba dang / phyag bya ba dang / thal mo sbyar bar byas pa dang / 
30b3(phal chen): rjes su spyon pa dang / spyan drangs pa dang / mchod pa dang / mngon du mthong ba dang dzum pa bya ba dang / sangs rgyas la dga' ba'i sems kyis mos par bye ba'i dge ba'i rtsa bo'i sgo nas kyang sa
30b4(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi srin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas rjes su dran par gyur pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sde
30b5(phal chen): rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas mthong bar 'dod par byas pas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi
30b6(phal chen): phrin las mdzad do// de bzhin ga shegs pa'i sku kha dog dang dbyibs kyi rnam pa tshad med pa bstan pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems ca rnams la sangs
30b7(phal chen): rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung thos par bya bas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad
30b8(phal chen): de// de dag la sogs pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rnam pa bye ba khrag khrag brgya stong brjod du med pa dag/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma la
31a1(phal chen): pa rnams cad du sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / mthu dang 'dul ba ji lta ba'i tshul las mi 'da' bar 'byung ngo // de ltar sangs rgyas kyi phrin las

33a7(phal chen): ngas ma ga togs par lha dang bcas pa'i 'angatan gyis tshad gzung bar ma nus so// 'das pa dang pa 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad
33a8(phal chen): 'jug par mi nus pa'o// kyergyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gnyis su med par spyod cing / dngos po rnam gnyis su med
33b1(phal chen): chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'deg ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni lung bstan pa rnams cad ston pa la gnyis su med par spyad do// sangs
33b2(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems ldan sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa la brtson pa rnams kyi sems dang bsam pa brjod du med pa 'bya ba klas pa mas la gnyis tha med par
33b3(phal chen): spyod do// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi don ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pas gnyis su med pa'i sku rnam par mdzod do// 'das pa dang mabyon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin
33b4(phal chen): shegs pa thams cad la rang bzhin gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// 'byung ba dang byung ba'i mtha' gnyis su med pa dang / sngon gyi mtha' dang da skur byung ba gnyis su
33b5(phal chen): med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad gnyis su med pas dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad gcig par rab tu mkhyen cing ston pa thugs su chud
33b6(phal chen): mnga' ba'o// sangs rgyas gcig dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsang gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis thugs su chud pa dang / 'du
33b7(phal chen): bamadzad pa'i rnam par dmigs su med par thugs su drad pa mnga'a'o// 'jig ted kyi chos thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos gnyis su med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// 'das
33b8(phal chen): byon pa dang ngas byung ba mangs ma thams cad byed ge pa'i rtsa thams cad dag pazhes pa ga // gnyis mad par rgyas pargyad pa mnga' ba sa// kye rgyal ba'i bras
34a1(phal chen): de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gnyis su med par spyod cing / dngos po gnyis su med pa'i chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos so// kye rgyal ba'i smras
34a2(phal chen): bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa btsugs po chos thams cad la rab tu zhugs pa rnams so// ji cu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
34a3(phal chen): 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i ye shes thugs su chud pal bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs rje chen po ma mnyam pa la bzhugs pa'o// 
34a4(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni smon lam ji ltab pazhin du 'byung ba la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'dul ba'i sems can yongs su mi gtong / 
34a5(phal chen): bal bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po med pa la gnas pa'i chos nyid la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de bzhin gshegs
34a6(phal chen): sru bskal ba mnyam pa tha mi dad cing don yod pa la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rtag tu mnyam par bzhag pa'i thugs la bzhugs pa'o// 
34a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad nyams pa med par gzhol ba la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i dgongs pa
34a8(phal chen): rnam par spyod pa la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas pacom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pas grub pa med pa'i yang dag pa'i mtha'i mtshan nyid
34b1(phal chen): bzhugs pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa chos thams cad la bzugs pa rnams so// kye rgyal ba
34b2(phal chen): sras bcu pa 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad ma lus par mngon par mkhyen pa rnams te/ bran gang zhen/ 'di sa ste/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pas
34b3(phal chen): cad kyi 'das pa bgrangs pa mdza' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / ma 'ongs pa bgrangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / de lur byung ba 'ablang rab mtha' nga
34b4(phal chen): mas cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / tshig gi lam mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / 'jig rten gyi rgyud mtha' dag thams cad mngon par ma byin pa dang / sems can gyi
34b5(phal chen): bsam pa dang shes pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba chung ngu dang 'bring dang chen po dang / rnam pa sna tshogs su rnam par gnas pa'i
34b6(phal chen): tshan nyid kyis dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams la bsam pa tshad med pa yongs su mi gtong bas sangs rgyas kyi ye shes 'bar bar bya ba dang / yongs su rdzogs par bya ba mtha' dag thams cad
34b7(phal chen): pa ma khyen pa dang / chas thams ca la ma ba'i mkhyen dum 'dag thams ca mngon pa martson pa dang / 'jig rten kyi spyod thams cad rnam par dbye ba'i mi shes gzigs man 'das
34b8(phal chen): thabs cad mngon par bya/ khyen pa dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi mig 'phrul kye rnam pa la bur dbye thams cad mngon par mkhyer pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs
35a1(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad ma lus par mkhyen pa'o// // bam po bzhi pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas ba
35a2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi stobs chen po// stobs dam pa stobs chad med pa stobs bdag nyid che ba spobs thug pa med pa thobs mi mnyam pa spobs snying po dang ldan pa/ stobs mi
35a3(phal chen): ge stobs 'jig rten thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ stobs sems can thams cad kyis mi 'phrog la/ sangs rgyas kyi rgyal mtshan stobs po che/ dpe' bo chen po'i sto
35a4(phal chen): rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi sku ni pha rol gyi gnod pa thams cad kyis mi shigs mi chod pa'o// 'jig rten gyi yul thams cad kyis sku tshe'i dbang po nyams pa
35a5(phal chen): rus pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi bskal po'i me'i gdung bas 'tshig par mi rus pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'jig par gtogs pa'i bu'i phung por 'grongs
35a6(phal chen): mi 'byung ba'o// bdud thams cad dang / bdud kyi sde thams cad dang / lha rnams cad kyi dpung dang / klu dang gnod sbyin dang dri na dpa l+h+wa ma yin dang nam mkha' lding dang ma 'am nI dang po
35a7(phal chen): bodong mi dang / me ma len pa thams cad kyi dpung dang / shaze dang / srin pa thams cad kyi dpung dang / sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi dpung gis bkol bar dga' 'a'o// ro rje rer
35a8(phal chen): nyes char pa dang / khor yug gi ri chen po tsam 'am/ stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i tsam gyi rdo rje'i char bab kyang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par
35b1(phal chen): rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi ba spu gcig kyang 'gul bar mi 'gyur/ g.yo bar mi 'gyur te/ bag tsha ba'i shes te yanga'o// bzhugs sam bzhengs sam bcud dam/ gzims kyang rlung ste/ s+ho/ 
35b2(phal chen): lam 'gyur ba med do// de bzhin gshegs pa gang na bzhugs pa'i yul de dang de'i 'khor dag du yang de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes na kun tu 'bab par mi 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi nam ro
35b3(phal chen): ba rnams la yang gnod par mi 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs pa'i sems can rnams lnga yang gnod par mi 'gyur zhi/ me g.yon de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la smos kyang ci
35b4(phal chen): dgos te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi stod pa'i rgyal ma tshan gyi chos dang po'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'ang
35b5(phal chen): kyis na/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyis klas pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ri rab kyi ri dang bcas pa/ khor lug dang khor yug chen po'i ri dang bcas pa/ rgya mtsho dang / ri dang nags tshal
35b6(phal chen): khas po dang / sems can gnas pa'i gnas tha dad pa kun dang / bcas pa de lu bu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i ba spu'i bu ga gcig tu btsud de/ bye ma'i mtha'
35b7(phal chen): skal pa'i yun zhugs par bzhag kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi brlabs pa gtogs par sems can rnams kyis shes par mi nus so// de bzhin gshegs pa de dag ni de snyed kyi 'dig
35b8(phal chen): kyi khams sku'i ba spu'i khung bu gcig gis bzung ste/ phyi ma'i mtha' ngaskal pa'i mar thug par bsdams shing / gshegs sam/ bzhugs sam/ bzhengs sam/ gzims kyang
36a1(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs skad cig tsam yang sgru ba mi mnga'o// chud cing drub par mi 'gyur ro// mthu dang stobs la yongs su nyas par 'gyur ba mi mnga'o// skun
36a2(phal chen): las rnam par 'gyur ba mi ma 'o// kyergyal ba'i sras 'di la sa dper mi nam mkha' ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'dzin kyang spro ba med do// 
36a3(phal chen): med do// gnod pa med do// med par mi 'gyur ro// mig ye ma 'brang mi 'jig go// de bzhin du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyang ba spu'i khung thug cig du 'jig
36a4(phal chen): ma lus pa tham pa bsnams kyang / de'i rgyus thugs skad cig tsam du yang mi bde ba'i sku nyams mi 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i
36a5(phal chen): stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi sbed pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos gnyis pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams gshegs stobs gcig tu bzhugs pas/ sangs rgyas
36a6(phal chen): deng brjod du med pa'i ya re brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi khams yongs su 'da' ning / dgongs pa bskyed pa gcig gis bskal pa tha dad pa'i rim par sangs rgyas
36a7(phal chen): nga brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba bsnyed 'byung ba mdzad do// de lta bur gshegs pas bskol pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu
36a8(phal chen): gshegs sheng/ 'jig rter kye khams thams cad kyi sems kyi/ de ji skyed pa'i bskum par bzhud de/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba srid / 'jig
36b1(phal chen): rten gyi khams tsam du 'khor kun du rgya che zhing yangs pa'i 'khor yug chen za' dranga'ang dang / sangs rgyas kyis ning gi rnam pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa la bsas bskyed
36b2(phal chen): la shin tu phra ba snyed kyang / de la bsres pa de snyed pa spu'i khung bu gcig tu btsud de/ spu'i khung bu gcig tu ji lu ba bzhin du/ sgra'i ba spu'i khung bu thams cad du btsud de/ ba spu'i khung bu
36b3(phal chen): yang sems can thams cad de snyed du gyur la/ de dag thams cad bsnams te/ de snyed kyi ba spu'i khung bu tshul de bzhin du bshams te/ thugs bskyed pa de su dras/ de bzhin gshegs pa
36b4(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gyu zhing gshegs sam/ phyogs kyi dra ba thams cad du rmya zhing gshegs sam/ nam mkha'i dbyings thams cad du rgyu ning gshegs sa ma/ 'jig rten
36b5(phal chen): rnyed 'grangs pa sngon gyi mtha gtogs pa nas bzung ste/ phye ma mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par/ de bzhin gshegs pas bskal pa thabs cid zad par gyur kyang de bzhin
36b6(phal chen): ba bzhud pa la brtson pa ni nyams par mi 'gyur ro// sku nyams myong bar mi 'gyur ro// dgongs pa rnams par 'khrug par mi 'gyur ro// ting nge 'dzin nyams par mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin
36b7(phal chen): gshegs pa'i sku yongs su nyams par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos gsum pa'o// 
36b8(phal chen): gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bsod snyoms gcig bzhes nas bskal pa brjod du med par skyil mo krung gcig bcas paso// nyin mtshan gyi rgyun tu sngon gyi mtha' dang / 
37a1(phal chen): phyi ma'i mtha'i phur gtogs pa'i bskal pa bzhugs kyang / sku mi g.yo zhing bde ba'i dam pa la spyod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa babam gyis
37a2(phal chen): byab par rnam par spyod kyang / sems can 'ga' tsam la yang sangs rgyas kyi phrin la sa rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku de la 'jig rten gyi khams thams ca
37a3(phal chen): yongs su bkod do// 'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi sems can gcig gi lus kyang 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba sbed tsam
37a4(phal chen): de lta bur gyur la/ sems can gcig gi lus kyi tshad ji tsam pa de ma gyi lus su sems can thams cad sbyar la/ sems can de dag re dong gzugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams
37a5(phal chen): cad kyi ljid ji tsam yod pa de tsam du skur te/ sems can gcig gi lci ba bzhin du sems can thams cad re re'i ltad kyang de tsam du gyur te/ sems can de dag thams cad de bzhin
37a6(phal chen): sa pa'i phyag song ki rtse mo gcig la/ phyi ng+ge'i mtha'i bskal pa'i bur chug par bsdabs te/ phyag sor gyi rtse mo gcig gis ji ltar bsnams pa dreng shin sugs
37a7(phal chen): la'ang/ de tsam dang bsnams kyang / de'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa sems nyi sa pa'am/ dgengs pa dub par mi 'gyung te/ thugs bskyed pa'i ma shes shid tu
37a8(phal chen): tsam du yang sduka bsngal mi bde ba skye bar mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams la 'jug pa dang / nam mkha' dbyed sa la 'jug pa dang / phyogs kyi
37b1(phal chen): rnamapa la 'jug pa dang del bu la 'jug pa nam mkha' khams ma lus pa'i dbyings kyis klas pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi mthar gzugs pa sgra'i rtse mo gnas pa'i 'ang
37b2(phal chen): na phyi khams la 'jug pa thams cad re re ning yang / skra'i rtse mo'i chags kyis gzhal te/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyis kun tu khyab pa thams cad ma lus pa'i sgra'i rtse ma'i cha shas
37b3(phal chen): kyis da mtha'i dbyings la 'jug pa thams cad du zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod lam 'di tshul dang / skyil mo krung gcig tu bzhugs pa'i spyod pas/ sngon
37b4(phal chen): mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' bur zug pa'i bskal pa zad par mdzad de/ bskal pa 'da' bar mdzad cing / bskal pa la rab tu 'jug ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ra
37b5(phal chen): 'u bo ma chen pa'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi sbed pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bzhi pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gcig la/ dbu sangs rgyas kyi
37b6(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rnam shin du phra bskyed byin gyis brlongs te/ dpung de yang lhag sa sangs rgyas kyi ning brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i du'o shes
37b7(phal chen): tu phra ba snyed byin gyis brlabs nas/ de dag re res kyang dbyangs kyi yan lag dang sgra skad kyi gsung / sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu pra ba
37b8(phal chen): dare re brjod de/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i sems can gyi khams
38a1(phal chen): zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bshad la mdo sde re re la yang chos bstan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du
38a2(phal chen): med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu gzhol bar mdzad de/ chos bstan pa gcig las kyang chos kyi tshil dang yi ge sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med
38a3(phal chen): rdul shin du phra ba snyed brjod par gyur la/ chos bstan pa gcig las ji lta ba de bzhin du chos bstan pa thams cad las kyang de snyed kyi chos kyi tshig dang yi ge brjod de/

38a5(phal chen): 'ad ba'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed zad par gyur kyang / da dung gzhan yang bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi nang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du brgyud cing rab tu ston pa'i tshu
38a6(phal chen): kyis rnam grangs 'dis bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdub shin tu phrab snyed du rab tu bstan la/ rnam grangs 'di 'dra bas bskal ba 'jig rten gyi khams
38a7(phal chen): thams cad kyi rdul shin tu dra ba snyed zadadra la sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi spyod pa snyed kyi bskal pa 'das par gyur te/ phyi ma'i mtha' mur thug pa'i bskal bzang
38a8(phal chen): nga 'das par byas kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa chos thams cad snang ba'i 'khor lo bar

38b5(phal chen): dpe 'id bang rab tu 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi rnam mkha'i dbyings kyi mapas gzugs pad+ma'i rtsema'achags

38b8(phal chen): rala'ang de skyed de skyed kyi dbu mnga' bar 'gyur la gzhung de bzhin du dbu re re la yang de skyed de skyed kyi sdug mnga' bar gyur te/ lcug re re las kyang de sred de skyed kyi dbyangs

39b2(phal chen): por 'jigs pa/ 'jigs pa chen po bskyed pa/ 'gro ba thams cad gsod pa/ 'jig rten thams cad phung bar byed pa de lta bu sha stag gis/ byang chub kyi shing drung dang / chos
39b3(phal chen): dbyings thams cad dang / nam mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thug par gang ba gzigs kyang byang chub kyi shing drung na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la bsrings pa mi ma / 
39b4(phal chen): bag tsha ba mi mnga' 'o// ba spu gcig kyang g.yo ba med do// dgongs pa'i cha shin tu phra ba 'gal tsam gyis kyang de ltar rnam pa tha dad pa'i gzugs la mtshan ma rnam pa tha dad 'dzin
